int	int
main	main
(	left_parenthesis
)	right_parenthesis
{	left_curly_bracket
a	var_name
=	equal
5	int_literal
;	semi_colon
b	var_name
=	equal
5	int_literal
;	semi_colon
c	var_name
=	equal
10	int_literal
;	semi_colon
d	var_name
=	equal
11	int_literal
;	semi_colon
a	var_name
=	equal
3	int_literal
+	arith_op
4	int_literal
;	semi_colon
if	if
(	left_parenthesis
a	var_name
==	rel_op
3	int_literal
)	right_parenthesis
{	left_curly_bracket
a	var_name
=	equal
0	int_literal
;	semi_colon
}	right_curly_bracket
while	while
(	left_parenthesis
b	var_name
>	rel_op
3	int_literal
)	right_parenthesis
{	left_curly_bracket
b	var_name
=	equal
b	var_name
-	arith_op
1	int_literal
;	semi_colon
}	right_curly_bracket
}	right_curly_bracket

*******TOKENS*******
Existen 4 tokens:
0:	 Nombre: a 	 Tipo:  	 Valor: 
1:	 Nombre: b 	 Tipo:  	 Valor: 
2:	 Nombre: c 	 Tipo:  	 Valor: 
3:	 Nombre: d 	 Tipo:  	 Valor:

[=, 10,  , c]
[=, 11,  , d]
[=, ,  , ]
[arith_op, CONSTANT, CONSTANT, T1]
[=, 0,  , a]
[rel_op, CONSTANT, var_name, T2]
[IFT, T0, GOTO L0]
[=, 0,  , a]
[=, 1,  , b]
[rel_op, CONSTANT, var_name, T3]
[LABEL, , , L1]
[=, 1,  , b]
[arith_op, CONSTANT, var_name, T4]
